posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:An old hotel with old facilities. Both advantages and disadvantages are obvious.
The advantage is that the hotel is in Yunlong Lake Scenic Area, which is very suitable for walking around when you bring the elderly.
The biggest disadvantage is that it is in Yunlong Lake Scenic Area. Daily travel is the biggest difficulty. The traffic jams are so severe during holidays. Every time you go out, you have to walk out for more than ten minutes to take a taxi. When you come back, you have to get off the car and walk back more than ten minutes in advance. It is very inconvenient to bring the elderly and children.
In addition, the king-size bed room is made of two small beds in the standard room. It is very uncomfortable to sleep in the middle.
For breakfast, you can enter at will without registration. So can I understand that you donâ€™t need to buy a room with breakfast at all? And there are very few breakfast categories, which are basically chain hotel standards, which are completely disproportionate to the room rate.
